## 🤖 Assistant

# 问题四：纯遗传算法实现无人机烟幕干扰弹投放优化

```python
import numpy as np
import random
from deap import base, creator, tools, algorithms
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import pandas as pd
import time

def optimize_with_genetic_algorithm():
    """
    使用纯遗传算法优化无人机烟幕弹投放策略
    """
    start_time = time.time()

    # 重置DEAP的创建器（如果之前已经定义过）
    if hasattr(creator, "FitnessMax"):
        del creator.FitnessMax
    if hasattr(creator, "Individual"):
        del creator.Individual

    # 定义初始位置
    FY1_initial_pos = (17800, 0, 1800)
    M1_initial_pos = (20000, 0, 2000)

    # 创建DEAP的适应度和个体类型
    creator.create("FitnessMax", base.Fitness, weights=(1.0,))
    creator.create("Individual", list, fitness=creator.FitnessMax)

    toolbox = base.Toolbox()

    # 定义参数基因
    # 方向角：控制无人机飞行方向
    toolbox.register("attr_azimuth", random.uniform, -np.pi / 10, np.pi / 10)
    # 速度：无人机飞行速度
    toolbox.register("attr_speed", random.uniform, 90, 120)
    # 投放时间1：第一枚烟幕弹投放时间
    toolbox.register("attr_release_time1", random.uniform, 0, 1)
    # 投放时间2：第二枚烟幕弹投放时间
    toolbox.register("attr_release_time2", random.uniform, 1, 5)
    # 投放时间3：第三枚烟幕弹投放时间
    toolbox.register("attr_release_time3", random.uniform, 5, 10)
    # 延迟时间1：第一枚烟幕弹爆炸延迟
    toolbox.register("attr_delay1", random.uniform, 0, 1)
    # 延迟时间2：第二枚烟幕弹爆炸延迟
    toolbox.register("attr_delay2", random.uniform, 0, 1)
    # 延迟时间3：第三枚烟幕弹爆炸延迟
    toolbox.register("attr_delay3", random.uniform, 0, 1)

    # 定义个体（染色体）
    toolbox.register(
        "individual",
        tools.initCycle,
        creator.Individual,
        (
            toolbox.attr_azimuth,
            toolbox.attr_speed,
            toolbox.attr_release_time1,
            toolbox.attr_delay1,
            toolbox.attr_release_time2,
            toolbox.attr_delay2,
            toolbox.attr_release_time3,
            toolbox.attr_delay3,
        ),
        n=1,
    )

    # 定义种群
    toolbox.register("population", tools.initRepeat, list, toolbox.individual)

    # 定义评估函数
    def evaluate(individual):
        """
        评估个体的适应度（总遮蔽时长）
        """
        # 解析基因参数
        azimuth, speed, release_time1, delay1, release_time2, delay2, release_time3, delay3 = individual

        # 计算飞行方向向量
        direction_x = np.cos(azimuth)
        direction_y = np.sin(azimuth)
        direction_z = 0  # 水平飞行
        direction = (direction_x, direction_y, direction_z)

        # 计算目标位置（无人机将飞往的方向）
        dir_norm = np.sqrt(direction_x**2 + direction_y**2)
        target_distance = 20000  # 足够远的目标点距离
        plane_target = (
            FY1_initial_pos[0] + direction_x / dir_norm * target_distance,
            FY1_initial_pos[1] + direction_y / dir_norm * target_distance,
            FY1_initial_pos[2],  # 保持高度不变
        )

        # 收集三枚烟幕弹的遮蔽区间
        total_shielding_periods = []

        # 计算每枚烟幕弹的遮蔽效果
        for release_time, delay in [
            (release_time1, delay1),
            (release_time2, delay2),
            (release_time3, delay3),
        ]:
            try:
                # 调用遮蔽时长计算函数
                _, shield_times = calculate_shielding_duration(
                    missile_initial_pos=M1_initial_pos,
                    missile_velocity=300,
                    missile_target=(0, 0, 0),  # 导弹目标为原点
                    plane_initial_pos=FY1_initial_pos,
                    plane_target=plane_target,
                    plane_speed=speed,
                    release_time=release_time,
                    explosion_delay=delay,
                    sample_points=100,  # 降低采样点数提高性能
                    time_step=0.05,     # 使用较大时间步长
                    verbose=False,      # 不输出详细信息
                )
                # 添加到总遮蔽区间列表
                total_shielding_periods.extend(shield_times)
            except Exception as e:
                # 出错时跳过（例如计算异常）
                pass

        # 如果没有有效遮蔽区间，返回0
        if not total_shielding_periods:
            return (0.0,)

        # 合并重叠的遮蔽时间段
        total_shielding_periods.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])  # 按开始时间排序
        merged_periods = [total_shielding_periods[0]]     # 初始化合并列表

        for current in total_shielding_periods[1:]:
            previous = merged_periods[-1]
            if current[0] <= previous[1]:  # 如果当前区间与前一个重叠
                # 合并区间：保留较早开始时间，选择较晚结束时间
                merged_periods[-1] = (previous[0], max(previous[1], current[1]))
            else:
                # 无重叠，添加新区间
                merged_periods.append(current)

        # 计算总遮蔽时长（所有区间长度之和）
        total_duration = sum(end - start for start, end in merged_periods)

        # 添加奖惩机制优化投放时间分布
        # 检查投放时间间隔
        time_gaps = [
            abs(release_time2 - release_time1),
            abs(release_time3 - release_time2)
        ]

        # 如果时间间隔太小，给予轻微惩罚
        for gap in time_gaps:
            if 0 < gap < 1.0:  # 间隔小于1秒
                total_duration *= 0.9  # 10%惩罚
            elif 1.0 <= gap < 2.0:  # 间隔在1-2秒之间
                total_duration *= 0.95  # 5%惩罚

        # 鼓励均匀分布的投放时间
        time_range = release_time3 - release_time1
        if time_range > 0 and len(time_gaps) > 0:
            evenness = min(time_gaps) / max(max(time_gaps), 0.001)  # 避免除零
            if evenness > 0.7:  # 比较均匀的分布
                total_duration *= 1.05  # 5%奖励

        return (total_duration,)

    # 注册评估函数
    toolbox.register("evaluate", evaluate)

    # 注册遗传操作
    # 交叉：融合参数
    toolbox.register("mate", tools.cxBlend, alpha=0.5)
    # 变异：高斯变异，根据参数重要性调整变异幅度
    toolbox.register(
        "mutate",
        tools.mutGaussian,
        mu=0,  # 均值为0
        sigma=[0.1, 3, 0.5, 0.2, 0.5, 0.2, 0.5, 0.2],  # 各参数变异幅度
        indpb=0.2,  # 每个基因变异概率
    )
    # 选择：锦标赛选择
    toolbox.register("select", tools.selTournament, tournsize=3)

    # 边界检查函数 - 确保所有参数在合理范围内
    def checkBounds():
        def decorator(func):
            def wrapper(*args, **kargs):
                offspring = func(*args, **kargs)

                for child in offspring:
                    # 方位角约束 [-π/10, π/10]
                    if child[0] > np.pi / 10:
                        child[0] = np.pi / 10
                    elif child[0] < -np.pi / 10:
                        child[0] = -np.pi / 10

                    # 飞行速度约束 [90, 120] m/s
                    if child[1] > 120:
                        child[1] = 120
                    elif child[1] < 90:
                        child[1] = 90

                    # 第一枚投放时间约束 [0, 1] s
                    if child[2] > 1:
                        child[2] = 1
                    elif child[2] < 0:
                        child[2] = 0

                    # 第一枚延迟约束 [0, 1] s
                    if child[3] > 1:
                        child[3] = 1
                    elif child[3] < 0:
                        child[3] = 0

                    # 第二枚投放时间约束 [1, 5] s
                    if child[4] > 5:
                        child[4] = 5
                    elif child[4] < 1:
                        child[4] = 1

                    # 第二枚延迟约束 [0, 1] s
                    if child[5] > 1:
                        child[5] = 1
                    elif child[5] < 0:
                        child[5] = 0

                    # 第三枚投放时间约束 [5, 10] s
                    if child[6] > 10:
                        child[6] = 10
                    elif child[6] < 5:
                        child[6] = 5

                    # 第三枚延迟约束 [0, 1] s
                    if child[7] > 1:
                        child[7] = 1
                    elif child[7] < 0:
                        child[7] = 0

                    # 确保投放时间递增：t1 < t2 < t3
                    if child[4] <= child[2]:  # 第二枚必须比第一枚晚
                        child[4] = child[2] + 0.5  # 增加至少0.5秒差距
                    if child[6] <= child[4]:  # 第三枚必须比第二枚晚
                        child[6] = child[4] + 0.5  # 增加至少0.5秒差距

                return offspring
            return wrapper
        return decorator

    # 应用边界检查
    toolbox.decorate("mate", checkBounds())
    toolbox.decorate("mutate", checkBounds())

    # 创建初始种群
    pop_size = 200  # 种群规模
    population = toolbox.population(n=pop_size)

    # 尝试使用拉丁超立方采样增加多样性
    try:
        from scipy.stats import qmc

        # 定义参数边界
        bounds = [
            (-np.pi/10, np.pi/10),  # 方位角
            (90, 120),              # 速度
            (0, 1),                 # 第一枚投放时间
            (0, 1),                 # 第一枚延迟
            (1, 5),                 # 第二枚投放时间
            (0, 1),                 # 第二枚延迟
            (5, 10),                # 第三枚投放时间
            (0, 1),                 # 第三枚延迟
        ]

        # 生成拉丁超立方采样点
        sampler = qmc.LatinHypercube(d=8)
        samples = sampler.random(n=pop_size//2)

        # 将样本缩放到实际参数范围
        for i, (low, high) in enumerate(bounds):
            samples[:, i] = low + (high - low) * samples[:, i]

        # 将生成的样本应用到初始种群的一部分
        for j in range(min(pop_size//2, len(samples))):
            for i in range(len(bounds)):
                population[j][i] = samples[j, i]

        # 确保投放时间递增
        for ind in population[:pop_size//2]:
            if ind[4] <= ind[2]:  # t2 > t1
                ind[4] = ind[2] + 0.5
            if ind[6] <= ind[4]:  # t3 > t2
                ind[6] = ind[4] + 0.5

        print("使用拉丁超立方采样增强种群多样性")
    except ImportError:
        print("未安装scipy，使用随机初始化")

    # 名人堂 - 记录最佳个体
    hof = tools.HallOfFame(5)  # 保存前5个最佳解

    # 统计信息记录器
    stats = tools.Statistics(lambda ind: ind.fitness.values)
    stats.register("avg", np.mean)
    stats.register("min", np.min)
    stats.register("max", np.max)
    stats.register("std", np.std)

    # 自适应参数函数
    def adaptive_mutation_rate(gen_idx, max_gen, base_rate=0.3):
        """动态调整变异率"""
        progress = gen_idx / max_gen
        # 早期高变异率探索，后期低变异率微调
        return base_rate * (1 - 0.7 * progress)

    # 自适应sigma函数
    def adaptive_sigma(gen_idx, max_gen, base_sigma):
        """动态调整变异幅度"""
        progress = gen_idx / max_gen
        return [s * (1 - 0.8 * progress) for s in base_sigma]

    # 手动实现遗传算法主循环，以支持自适应参数
    generations = 100  # 总代数
    pop = population.copy()
    logbook = tools.Logbook()
    logbook.header = ["gen", "nevals"] + stats.fields if stats else []

    # 用于记录演化停滞的计数器
    stagnation_counter = 0
    best_fitness_history = []

    # 记录最佳个体
    best_ever = None
    best_fitness = 0

    print(f"开始遗传算法优化，种群大小={pop_size}，代数={generations}")

    # 主循环
    for gen in range(generations):
        # 自适应参数
        current_mutpb = adaptive_mutation_rate(gen, generations)
        current_sigma = adaptive_sigma(
            gen, generations,
            [0.1, 3, 0.5, 0.2, 0.5, 0.2, 0.5, 0.2]
        )

        # 选择
        offspring = toolbox.select(pop, len(pop))
        offspring = list(map(toolbox.clone, offspring))

        # 应用交叉
        for i in range(1, len(offspring), 2):
            if random.random() < 0.7:  # 交叉概率
                offspring[i-1], offspring[i] = toolbox.mate(offspring[i-1], offspring[i])
                del offspring[i-1].fitness.values
                del offspring[i].fitness.values

        # 应用变异
        for i in range(len(offspring)):
            if random.random() < current_mutpb:
                # 临时修改变异幅度
                old_sigma = toolbox.mutate.keywords["sigma"]
                toolbox.mutate.keywords["sigma"] = current_sigma
                offspring[i], = toolbox.mutate(offspring[i])
                # 恢复原始sigma
                toolbox.mutate.keywords["sigma"] = old_sigma
                del offspring[i].fitness.values

        # 评估新个体
        invalid_ind = [ind for ind in offspring if not ind.fitness.valid]
        fitnesses = map(toolbox.evaluate, invalid_ind)
        for ind, fit in zip(invalid_ind, fitnesses):
            ind.fitness.values = fit

        # 精英保留策略
        if gen > 0:
            # 找出上一代中的最佳个体
            best_idx = np.argmax([ind.fitness.values[0] for ind in pop])
            best_prev_gen = pop[best_idx]

            # 检查当前最佳个体是否比上一代最佳个体更好
            if max([ind.fitness.values[0] for ind in offspring]) < best_prev_gen.fitness.values[0]:
                # 如果没有更好的，保留上一代最佳个体
                worst_idx = np.argmin([ind.fitness.values[0] for ind in offspring])
                offspring[worst_idx] = toolbox.clone(best_prev_gen)

        # 更新种群
        pop[:] = offspring

        # 更新最佳个体记录
        current_best = max(pop, key=lambda x: x.fitness.values[0])
        current_best_fitness = current_best.fitness.values[0]
        best_fitness_history.append(current_best_fitness)

        if current_best_fitness > best_fitness:
            best_fitness = current_best_fitness
            best_ever = toolbox.clone(current_best)
            stagnation_counter = 0
        else:
            stagnation_counter += 1

        # 更新名人堂
        hof.update(pop)

        # 记录统计信息
        record = stats.compile(pop)
        logbook.record(gen=gen, nevals=len(invalid_ind), **record)

        # 每10代打印一次进度
        if gen % 10 == 0 or gen == generations - 1:
            print(f"第{gen}代: 最大适应度={record['max']:.4f}, 平均={record['avg']:.4f}")

        # 检测停滞并进行重启
        if stagnation_counter >= 15:
            print(f"检测到停滞，重新初始化30%种群...")
            # 找出表现最差的30%个体
            num_to_replace = int(0.3 * len(pop))
            worst_indices = np.argsort([ind.fitness.values[0] for ind in pop])[:num_to_replace]

            # 用新随机个体替换
            for idx in worst_indices:
                pop[idx] = toolbox.individual()
                pop[idx].fitness.values = toolbox.evaluate(pop[idx])

            # 重置停滞计数器
            stagnation_counter = 0

    # 使用最佳解
    best_ind = best_ever if best_ever and best_fitness > hof[0].fitness.values[0] else hof[0]

    # 解析最佳参数
    azimuth, speed, release_time1, delay1, release_time2, delay2, release_time3, delay3 = best_ind

    # 计算飞行方向
    direction_x = np.cos(azimuth)
    direction_y = np.sin(azimuth)
    direction_z = 0
    direction = (direction_x, direction_y, direction_z)

    # 计算飞行目标位置
    dir_norm = np.sqrt(direction_x**2 + direction_y**2)
    target_distance = 20000
    plane_target = (
        FY1_initial_pos[0] + direction_x / dir_norm * target_distance,
        FY1_initial_pos[1] + direction_y / dir_norm * target_distance,
        FY1_initial_pos[2],
    )

    # 角度转换（0-360度）
    direction_angle = (np.arctan2(direction_y, direction_x) * 180 / np.pi) % 360

    # 计算每枚烟幕弹详细参数
    bombs_data = []
    for idx, (release_time, explosion_delay) in enumerate([
        (release_time1, delay1),
        (release_time2, delay2),
        (release_time3, delay3),
    ]):
        # 投放点
        release_position = calculate_plane_position(
            FY1_initial_pos, direction, speed, release_time
        )

        # 起爆点
        explosion_position = calculate_bomb_position(
            FY1_initial_pos, direction, speed, release_time, explosion_delay
        )

        # 单枚干扰时长（高精度评估）
        duration, _ = calculate_shielding_duration(
            missile_initial_pos=M1_initial_pos,
            missile_velocity=300,
            missile_target=(0, 0, 0),
            plane_initial_pos=FY1_initial_pos,
            plane_target=plane_target,
            plane_speed=speed,
            release_time=release_time,
            explosion_delay=explosion_delay,
            sample_points=500,  # 提高精度
            verbose=False,
        )

        # 记录烟幕弹数据
        bombs_data.append({
            "编号": idx + 1,
            "运动方向": direction_angle,
            "运动速度": speed,
            "投放点x": release_position[0],
            "投放点y": release_position[1],
            "投放点z": release_position[2],
            "起爆点x": explosion_position[0],
            "起爆点y": explosion_position[1],
            "起爆点z": explosion_position[2],
            "有效干扰时长": duration,
        })

    # 计算总有效干扰时长（高精度评估）
    total_shielding_periods = []
    for release_time, explosion_delay in [
        (release_time1, delay1),
        (release_time2, delay2),
        (release_time3, delay3),
    ]:
        _, shield_times = calculate_shielding_duration(
            missile_initial_pos=M1_initial_pos,
            missile_velocity=300,
            missile_target=(0, 0, 0),
            plane_initial_pos=FY1_initial_pos,
            plane_target=plane_target,
            plane_speed=speed,
            release_time=release_time,
            explosion_delay=explosion_delay,
            sample_points=500,
            verbose=False,
        )
        total_shielding_periods.extend(shield_times)

    # 合并重叠区间
    if total_shielding_periods:
        total_shielding_periods.sort(key=lambda x: x[0])
        merged_periods = [total_shielding_periods[0]]

        for current in total_shielding_periods[1:]:
            previous = merged_periods[-1]
            if current[0] <= previous[1]:
                merged_periods[-1] = (previous[0], max(previous[1], current[1]))
            else:
                merged_periods.append(current)

        total_duration = sum(end - start for start, end in merged_periods)
    else:
        total_duration = 0.0
        merged_periods = []

    # 创建结果DataFrame
    df = pd.DataFrame(columns=[
        "无人机运动方向",
        "无人机运动速度 (m/s)",
        "烟幕干扰弹编号",
        "烟幕干扰弹投放点的x坐标 (m)",
        "烟幕干扰弹投放点的y坐标 (m)",
        "烟幕干扰弹投放点的z坐标 (m)",
        "烟幕干扰弹起爆点的x坐标 (m)",
        "烟幕干扰弹起爆点的y坐标 (m)",
        "烟幕干扰弹起爆点的z坐标 (m)",
        "有效干扰时长 (s)",
    ])

    # 填充数据
    for i, bomb in enumerate(bombs_data):
        df.loc[i] = [
            bomb["运动方向"],
            bomb["运动速度"],
            bomb["编号"],
            bomb["投放点x"], bomb["投放点y"], bomb["投放点z"],
            bomb["起爆点x"], bomb["起爆点y"], bomb["起爆点z"],
            bomb["有效干扰时长"],
        ]

    # 保存到Excel
    result_file = "result4.xlsx"
    df.to_excel(result_file, index=False)
    print(f"结果已保存到{result_file}")

    # 输出优化结果
    print("\n=== 优化结果 ===")
    print(f"无人机运动方向: {direction_angle:.2f}度")
    print(f"无人机运动速度: {speed:.2f} m/s")
    print(f"总有效干扰时长: {total_duration:.4f}秒")
    print(f"烟幕弹1: 投放时间={release_time1:.2f}s, 延迟={delay1:.2f}s, 干扰时长={bombs_data[0]['有效干扰时长']:.2f}s")
    print(f"烟幕弹2: 投放时间={release_time2:.2f}s, 延迟={delay2:.2f}s, 干扰时长={bombs_data[1]['有效干扰时长']:.2f}s")
    print(f"烟幕弹3: 投放时间={release_time3:.2f}s, 延迟={delay3:.2f}s, 干扰时长={bombs_data[2]['有效干扰时长']:.2f}s")

    # 计算优化耗时
    end_time = time.time()
    elapsed_time = end_time - start_time
    print(f"优化总耗时: {elapsed_time:.2f}秒")

    # 绘制进化过程图
    gen = range(len(logbook))
    if 'avg' in logbook.chapters:
        avg = logbook.select("avg")
        max_fit = logbook.select("max")

        plt.figure(figsize=(10, 6))
        plt.plot(gen, avg, label="平均适应度")
        plt.plot(gen, max_fit, label="最大适应度")
        plt.xlabel("代数")
        plt.ylabel("适应度(总遮蔽时长)")
        plt.legend()
        plt.title("问题四遗传算法优化进程")
        plt.grid(True)
        plt.savefig("GA优化进程.png", dpi=300)
        plt.show()

    # 返回结果
    return best_ind, bombs_data, total_duration, merged_periods


def run_optimization():
    """运行遗传算法优化"""
    # 设置随机种子确保可重现性
    random.seed(42)
    np.random.seed(42)

    try:
        # 运行优化
        best_params, bombs_data, total_duration, shield_periods = optimize_with_genetic_algorithm()
        print(f"\n优化成功完成！最大总遮蔽时长: {total_duration:.4f}秒")

        # 可以在这里添加结果可视化代码

    except Exception as e:
        print(f"优化过程中出错: {e}")
        import traceback
        traceback.print_exc()


# 主函数
if __name__ == "__main__":
    run_optimization()
```

## 纯遗传算法方法的主要特点和优势

1. **自适应参数策略**

- 随着进化进程动态调整变异率和变异幅度
- 初期高变异率促进探索，后期低变异率保护好的解

2. **多样性增强机制**

- 使用拉丁超立方采样生成初始种群，确保参数空间覆盖均匀
- 检测进化停滞并重
